33 // Return an RI instruction like MI with opcode Opcode, but with the ----
34 // GR64 register operands turned into GR32s. ----
35 static MCInst lowerRILow(const MachineInstr *MI, unsigned Opcode) { 0
36 if (MI->isCompare()) 0
37 return MCInstBuilder(Opcode) 0
38 .addReg(SystemZMC::getRegAsGR32(MI->getOperand(0).getReg())) 0
39 .addImm(MI->getOperand(1).getImm()); 0
40 else ----
41 return MCInstBuilder(Opcode) 0
42 .addReg(SystemZMC::getRegAsGR32(MI->getOperand(0).getReg())) 0
43 .addReg(SystemZMC::getRegAsGR32(MI->getOperand(1).getReg())) 0
44 .addImm(MI->getOperand(2).getImm()); 0
45 } ----

61 // Return an RI instruction like MI with opcode Opcode, but with the ----

87 // MI is an instruction that accepts an optional alignment hint, ----
88 // and which was already lowered to LoweredMI. If the alignment ----
89 // of the original memory operand is known, update LoweredMI to ----
90 // an instruction with the corresponding hint set. ----
91 static void lowerAlignmentHint(const MachineInstr *MI, MCInst &LoweredMI, 0
92 unsigned Opcode) { ----
93 if (MI->memoperands_empty()) 0
94 return; 0
95 ----
96 Align Alignment = Align(16); 0
97 for (MachineInstr::mmo_iterator MMOI = MI->memoperands_begin(), 0
98 EE = MI->memoperands_end(); MMOI != EE; ++MMOI) 0
99 if ((*MMOI)->getAlign() < Alignment) 0
100 Alignment = (*MMOI)->getAlign(); 0
101 ----
102 unsigned AlignmentHint = 0; 0
103 if (Alignment >= Align(16)) 0
104 AlignmentHint = 4; 0
105 else if (Alignment >= Align(8)) 0
106 AlignmentHint = 3; 0
107 if (AlignmentHint == 0) 0
108 return; 0
109 ----
110 LoweredMI.setOpcode(Opcode); 0
111 LoweredMI.addOperand(MCOperand::createImm(AlignmentHint)); 0
112 } ----

114 // MI loads the high part of a vector from memory. Return an instruction ----
115 // that uses replicating vector load Opcode to do the same thing. ----
116 static MCInst lowerSubvectorLoad(const MachineInstr *MI, unsigned Opcode) { 0
117 return MCInstBuilder(Opcode) 0
118 .addReg(SystemZMC::getRegAsVR128(MI->getOperand(0).getReg())) 0
119 .addReg(MI->getOperand(1).getReg()) 0
120 .addImm(MI->getOperand(2).getImm()) 0
121 .addReg(MI->getOperand(3).getReg()); 0
122 } ----
123 ----
124 // MI stores the high part of a vector to memory. Return an instruction ----
125 // that uses elemental vector store Opcode to do the same thing. ----
126 static MCInst lowerSubvectorStore(const MachineInstr *MI, unsigned Opcode) { 0
127 return MCInstBuilder(Opcode) 0

130 .addImm(MI->getOperand(2).getImm()) 0
131 .addReg(MI->getOperand(3).getReg()) 0
132 .addImm(0); 0
133 } ----

135 // The XPLINK ABI requires that a no-op encoding the call type is emitted after ----
136 // each call to a subroutine. This information can be used by the called ----
137 // function to determine its entry point, e.g. for generating a backtrace. The ----
138 // call type is encoded as a register number in the bcr instruction. See ----
139 // enumeration CallType for the possible values. ----
140 void SystemZAsmPrinter::emitCallInformation(CallType CT) { 0
141 EmitToStreamer(*OutStreamer, 0
142 MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::BCRAsm) 0
143 .addImm(0) 0
144 .addReg(SystemZMC::GR64Regs[static_cast(CT)])); 0
145 } 0

147 uint32_t SystemZAsmPrinter::AssociatedDataAreaTable::insert(const MCSymbol *Sym, 0
148 unsigned SlotKind) { ----
149 auto Key = std::make_pair(Sym, SlotKind); 0
150 auto It = Displacements.find(Key); 0
151 ----
152 if (It != Displacements.end()) 0
153 return (*It).second; 0
154 ----
155 // Determine length of descriptor. ----
156 uint32_t Length; ----
157 switch (SlotKind) { 0
158 case SystemZII::MO_ADA_DIRECT_FUNC_DESC: 0
159 Length = 2 * PointerSize; 0
160 break; 0
161 default: 0
162 Length = PointerSize; 0
163 break; 0
164 } ----
165 ----
166 uint32_t Displacement = NextDisplacement; 0
167 Displacements[std::make_pair(Sym, SlotKind)] = NextDisplacement; 0
168 NextDisplacement += Length; 0
169 ----
170 return Displacement; 0
171 } ----

173 uint32_t ----
174 SystemZAsmPrinter::AssociatedDataAreaTable::insert(const MachineOperand MO) { 0
175 MCSymbol *Sym; ----
176 if (MO.getType() == MachineOperand::MO_GlobalAddress) { 0
177 const GlobalValue *GV = MO.getGlobal(); 0
178 Sym = MO.getParent()->getMF()->getTarget().getSymbol(GV); 0
179 assert(Sym && "No symbol"); 0
180 } else if (MO.getType() == MachineOperand::MO_ExternalSymbol) { 0
181 const char *SymName = MO.getSymbolName(); 0
182 Sym = MO.getParent()->getMF()->getContext().getOrCreateSymbol(SymName); 0
183 assert(Sym && "No symbol"); 0
184 } else ----
185 llvm_unreachable("Unexpected operand type"); 0
186 ----
187 unsigned ADAslotType = MO.getTargetFlags(); 0
188 return insert(Sym, ADAslotType); 0
189 } ----

586 LOWER_LOW(XILF); 0
587 ----
588 #undef LOWER_LOW ----
589 ----
590 #define LOWER_HIGH(NAME) \ ----
591 case SystemZ::NAME##64: LoweredMI = lowerRIHigh(MI, SystemZ::NAME); break ----
592 ----
593 LOWER_HIGH(IIHL); 0
594 LOWER_HIGH(IIHH); 0
595 LOWER_HIGH(TMHL); 0
596 LOWER_HIGH(TMHH); 0
597 LOWER_HIGH(NIHL); 0
598 LOWER_HIGH(NIHH); 0
599 LOWER_HIGH(NIHF); 0
600 LOWER_HIGH(OIHL); 0
601 LOWER_HIGH(OIHH); 0
602 LOWER_HIGH(OIHF); 0
603 LOWER_HIGH(XIHF); 0
604 ----
605 #undef LOWER_HIGH ----
606 ----
607 case SystemZ::Serialize: 0
608 if (MF->getSubtarget().hasFastSerialization()) 0
609 LoweredMI = MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::BCRAsm) 0
610 .addImm(14).addReg(SystemZ::R0D); 0
611 else ----
612 LoweredMI = MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::BCRAsm) 0
613 .addImm(15).addReg(SystemZ::R0D); 0
614 break; 0
615 ----
616 // We want to emit "j .+2" for traps, jumping to the relative immediate field ----
617 // of the jump instruction, which is an illegal instruction. We cannot emit a ----
618 // "." symbol, so create and emit a temp label before the instruction and use ----
619 // that instead. ----
620 case SystemZ::Trap: { 0
621 MCSymbol *DotSym = OutContext.createTempSymbol(); 0
622 OutStreamer->emitLabel(DotSym); 0
623 ----
624 const MCSymbolRefExpr *Expr = MCSymbolRefExpr::create(DotSym, OutContext); 0
625 const MCConstantExpr *ConstExpr = MCConstantExpr::create(2, OutContext); 0
626 LoweredMI = MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::J) 0
627 .addExpr(MCBinaryExpr::createAdd(Expr, ConstExpr, OutContext)); 0
628 } ----
629 break; 0
630 ----
631 // Conditional traps will create a branch on condition instruction that jumps ----
632 // to the relative immediate field of the jump instruction. (eg. "jo .+2") ----
633 case SystemZ::CondTrap: { 0
634 MCSymbol *DotSym = OutContext.createTempSymbol(); 0
635 OutStreamer->emitLabel(DotSym); 0
636 ----
637 const MCSymbolRefExpr *Expr = MCSymbolRefExpr::create(DotSym, OutContext); 0
638 const MCConstantExpr *ConstExpr = MCConstantExpr::create(2, OutContext); 0
639 LoweredMI = MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::BRC) 0
640 .addImm(MI->getOperand(0).getImm()) 0
641 .addImm(MI->getOperand(1).getImm()) 0
642 .addExpr(MCBinaryExpr::createAdd(Expr, ConstExpr, OutContext)); 0
643 } ----
644 break; 0
645 ----
646 case TargetOpcode::FENTRY_CALL: 0
647 LowerFENTRY_CALL(*MI, Lower); 0
648 return; 0
649 ----
650 case TargetOpcode::STACKMAP: 0
651 LowerSTACKMAP(*MI); 0
652 return; 0
653 ----
654 case TargetOpcode::PATCHPOINT: 0
655 LowerPATCHPOINT(*MI, Lower); 0
656 return; 0
657 ----
658 case SystemZ::EXRL_Pseudo: { 0
659 unsigned TargetInsOpc = MI->getOperand(0).getImm(); 0
660 Register LenMinus1Reg = MI->getOperand(1).getReg(); 0
661 Register DestReg = MI->getOperand(2).getReg(); 0
662 int64_t DestDisp = MI->getOperand(3).getImm(); 0
663 Register SrcReg = MI->getOperand(4).getReg(); 0
664 int64_t SrcDisp = MI->getOperand(5).getImm(); 0
665 ----
666 SystemZTargetStreamer *TS = getTargetStreamer(); 0
667 MCSymbol *DotSym = nullptr; 0
668 MCInst ET = MCInstBuilder(TargetInsOpc).addReg(DestReg) 0
669 .addImm(DestDisp).addImm(1).addReg(SrcReg).addImm(SrcDisp); 0
670 SystemZTargetStreamer::MCInstSTIPair ET_STI(ET, &MF->getSubtarget()); 0
671 SystemZTargetStreamer::EXRLT2SymMap::iterator I = ----
672 TS->EXRLTargets2Sym.find(ET_STI); 0
673 if (I != TS->EXRLTargets2Sym.end()) 0
674 DotSym = I->second; 0
675 else ----
676 TS->EXRLTargets2Sym[ET_STI] = DotSym = OutContext.createTempSymbol(); 0
677 const MCSymbolRefExpr *Dot = MCSymbolRefExpr::create(DotSym, OutContext); 0
678 EmitToStreamer( 0
679 *OutStreamer, 0
680 MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::EXRL).addReg(LenMinus1Reg).addExpr(Dot)); 0
681 return; 0
682 } 0
683 ----
684 default: 0
685 Lower.lower(MI, LoweredMI); 0
686 break; 0
687 } ----
688 EmitToStreamer(*OutStreamer, LoweredMI); 0
689 } 0
690 ----
691 // Emit the largest nop instruction smaller than or equal to NumBytes ----
692 // bytes. Return the size of nop emitted. ----
693 static unsigned EmitNop(MCContext &OutContext, MCStreamer &OutStreamer, 0
694 unsigned NumBytes, const MCSubtargetInfo &STI) { ----
695 if (NumBytes < 2) { 0
696 llvm_unreachable("Zero nops?"); 0
697 return 0; ----
698 } ----
699 else if (NumBytes < 4) { 0
700 OutStreamer.emitInstruction( 0
701 MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::BCRAsm).addImm(0).addReg(SystemZ::R0D), STI); 0
702 return 2; 0
703 } ----
704 else if (NumBytes < 6) { 0
705 OutStreamer.emitInstruction( 0
706 MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::BCAsm).addImm(0).addReg(0).addImm(0).addReg(0), 0
707 STI); ----
708 return 4; 0
709 } ----
710 else { ----
711 MCSymbol *DotSym = OutContext.createTempSymbol(); 0
712 const MCSymbolRefExpr *Dot = MCSymbolRefExpr::create(DotSym, OutContext); 0
713 OutStreamer.emitLabel(DotSym); 0
714 OutStreamer.emitInstruction( 0
715 MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::BRCLAsm).addImm(0).addExpr(Dot), STI); 0
716 return 6; 0
717 } ----
718 } ----
719 ----
720 void SystemZAsmPrinter::LowerFENTRY_CALL(const MachineInstr &MI, 0
721 SystemZMCInstLower &Lower) { ----
722 MCContext &Ctx = MF->getContext(); 0
723 if (MF->getFunction().hasFnAttribute("mrecord-mcount")) { 0
724 MCSymbol *DotSym = OutContext.createTempSymbol(); 0
725 OutStreamer->pushSection(); 0
726 OutStreamer->switchSection( 0
727 Ctx.getELFSection("__mcount_loc", ELF::SHT_PROGBITS, ELF::SHF_ALLOC)); 0
728 OutStreamer->emitSymbolValue(DotSym, 8); 0
729 OutStreamer->popSection(); 0
730 OutStreamer->emitLabel(DotSym); 0
731 } ----
732 ----
733 if (MF->getFunction().hasFnAttribute("mnop-mcount")) { 0
734 EmitNop(Ctx, *OutStreamer, 6, getSubtargetInfo()); 0
735 return; 0
736 } ----
737 ----
738 MCSymbol *fentry = Ctx.getOrCreateSymbol("__fentry__"); 0
739 const MCSymbolRefExpr *Op = ----
740 MCSymbolRefExpr::create(fentry, MCSymbolRefExpr::VK_PLT, Ctx); 0
741 OutStreamer->emitInstruction( 0
742 MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::BRASL).addReg(SystemZ::R0D).addExpr(Op), 0
743 getSubtargetInfo()); ----
744 } ----
745 ----
746 void SystemZAsmPrinter::LowerSTACKMAP(const MachineInstr &MI) { 0
747 auto *TII = MF->getSubtarget().getInstrInfo(); 0
748 ----
749 unsigned NumNOPBytes = MI.getOperand(1).getImm(); 0
750 ----
751 auto &Ctx = OutStreamer->getContext(); 0
752 MCSymbol *MILabel = Ctx.createTempSymbol(); 0
753 OutStreamer->emitLabel(MILabel); 0
754 ----
755 SM.recordStackMap(*MILabel, MI); 0
756 assert(NumNOPBytes % 2 == 0 && "Invalid number of NOP bytes requested!"); 0
757 ----
758 // Scan ahead to trim the shadow. ----
759 unsigned ShadowBytes = 0; 0
760 const MachineBasicBlock &MBB = *MI.getParent(); 0
761 MachineBasicBlock::const_iterator MII(MI); 0
762 ++MII; 0
763 while (ShadowBytes < NumNOPBytes) { 0
764 if (MII == MBB.end() || 0
765 MII->getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::PATCHPOINT || 0
766 MII->getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::STACKMAP) 0
767 break; 0
768 ShadowBytes += TII->getInstSizeInBytes(*MII); 0
769 if (MII->isCall()) 0
770 break; 0
771 ++MII; 0
772 } ----
773 ----
774 // Emit nops. ----
775 while (ShadowBytes < NumNOPBytes) 0
776 ShadowBytes += EmitNop(OutContext, *OutStreamer, NumNOPBytes - ShadowBytes, 0
777 getSubtargetInfo()); ----
778 } 0
779 ----
780 // Lower a patchpoint of the form: ----
781 // [], , , , ----
782 void SystemZAsmPrinter::LowerPATCHPOINT(const MachineInstr &MI, 0
783 SystemZMCInstLower &Lower) { ----
784 auto &Ctx = OutStreamer->getContext(); 0
785 MCSymbol *MILabel = Ctx.createTempSymbol(); 0
786 OutStreamer->emitLabel(MILabel); 0
787 ----
788 SM.recordPatchPoint(*MILabel, MI); 0
789 PatchPointOpers Opers(&MI); 0
790 ----
791 unsigned EncodedBytes = 0; 0
792 const MachineOperand &CalleeMO = Opers.getCallTarget(); 0
793 ----
794 if (CalleeMO.isImm()) { 0
795 uint64_t CallTarget = CalleeMO.getImm(); 0
796 if (CallTarget) { 0
797 unsigned ScratchIdx = -1; 0
798 unsigned ScratchReg = 0; 0
799 do { ----
800 ScratchIdx = Opers.getNextScratchIdx(ScratchIdx + 1); 0
801 ScratchReg = MI.getOperand(ScratchIdx).getReg(); 0
802 } while (ScratchReg == SystemZ::R0D); 0
803 ----
804 // Materialize the call target address ----
805 EmitToStreamer(*OutStreamer, MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::LLILF) 0
806 .addReg(ScratchReg) 0
807 .addImm(CallTarget & 0xFFFFFFFF)); 0
808 EncodedBytes += 6; 0
809 if (CallTarget >> 32) { 0
810 EmitToStreamer(*OutStreamer, MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::IIHF) 0
811 .addReg(ScratchReg) 0
812 .addImm(CallTarget >> 32)); 0
813 EncodedBytes += 6; 0
814 } ----
815 ----
816 EmitToStreamer(*OutStreamer, MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::BASR) 0
817 .addReg(SystemZ::R14D) 0
818 .addReg(ScratchReg)); 0
819 EncodedBytes += 2; 0
820 } ----
821 } else if (CalleeMO.isGlobal()) { 0
822 const MCExpr *Expr = Lower.getExpr(CalleeMO, MCSymbolRefExpr::VK_PLT); 0
823 EmitToStreamer(*OutStreamer, MCInstBuilder(SystemZ::BRASL) 0
824 .addReg(SystemZ::R14D) 0
825 .addExpr(Expr)); 0
826 EncodedBytes += 6; 0
827 } ----
828 ----
829 // Emit padding. ----
830 unsigned NumBytes = Opers.getNumPatchBytes(); 0
831 assert(NumBytes >= EncodedBytes && 0
832 "Patchpoint can't request size less than the length of a call."); ----
833 assert((NumBytes - EncodedBytes) % 2 == 0 && 0
834 "Invalid number of NOP bytes requested!"); ----
835 while (EncodedBytes < NumBytes) 0
836 EncodedBytes += EmitNop(OutContext, *OutStreamer, NumBytes - EncodedBytes, 0
837 getSubtargetInfo()); ----
838 } 0
839 ----
840 // The *alignment* of 128-bit vector types is different between the software ----
841 // and hardware vector ABIs. If the there is an externally visible use of a ----
842 // vector type in the module it should be annotated with an attribute. ----
843 void SystemZAsmPrinter::emitAttributes(Module &M) { 0
844 if (M.getModuleFlag("s390x-visible-vector-ABI")) { 0
845 bool HasVectorFeature = ----
846 TM.getMCSubtargetInfo()->hasFeature(SystemZ::FeatureVector); 0
847 OutStreamer->emitGNUAttribute(8, HasVectorFeature ? 2 : 1); 0
848 } ----
849 } 0
850 ----
851 // Convert a SystemZ-specific constant pool modifier into the associated ----
852 // MCSymbolRefExpr variant kind. ----
853 static MCSymbolRefExpr::VariantKind ----
854 getModifierVariantKind(SystemZCP::SystemZCPModifier Modifier) { 0
855 switch (Modifier) { 0
856 case SystemZCP::TLSGD: return MCSymbolRefExpr::VK_TLSGD; 0
857 case SystemZCP::TLSLDM: return MCSymbolRefExpr::VK_TLSLDM; 0
858 case SystemZCP::DTPOFF: return MCSymbolRefExpr::VK_DTPOFF; 0
859 case SystemZCP::NTPOFF: return MCSymbolRefExpr::VK_NTPOFF; 0
860 } ----
861 llvm_unreachable("Invalid SystemCPModifier!"); 0
862 } ----
863 ----
864 void SystemZAsmPrinter::emitMachineConstantPoolValue( 0
865 MachineConstantPoolValue *MCPV) { ----
866 auto *ZCPV = static_cast(MCPV); 0
867 ----
868 const MCExpr *Expr = ----
869 MCSymbolRefExpr::create(getSymbol(ZCPV->getGlobalValue()), 0
870 getModifierVariantKind(ZCPV->getModifier()), 0
871 OutContext); ----
872 uint64_t Size = getDataLayout().getTypeAllocSize(ZCPV->getType()); 0
873 ----
874 OutStreamer->emitValue(Expr, Size); 0
875 } 0
876 ----
877 static void printFormattedRegName(const MCAsmInfo *MAI, unsigned RegNo, 0
878 raw_ostream &OS) { ----
879 const char *RegName = SystemZInstPrinter::getRegisterName(RegNo); 0
880 if (MAI->getAssemblerDialect() == AD_HLASM) { 0
881 // Skip register prefix so that only register number is left ----
882 assert(isalpha(RegName[0]) && isdigit(RegName[1])); 0
883 OS << (RegName + 1); 0
884 } else ----
885 OS << '%' << RegName; 0
886 } 0
887 ----
888 static void printOperand(const MCOperand &MCOp, const MCAsmInfo *MAI, 0
889 raw_ostream &OS) { ----
890 if (MCOp.isReg()) { 0
891 if (!MCOp.getReg()) 0
892 OS << '0'; 0
893 else ----
894 printFormattedRegName(MAI, MCOp.getReg(), OS); 0
895 } else if (MCOp.isImm()) 0
896 OS << MCOp.getImm(); 0
897 else if (MCOp.isExpr()) 0
898 MCOp.getExpr()->print(OS, MAI); 0
899 else ----
900 llvm_unreachable("Invalid operand"); 0
901 } 0
902 ----
903 static void printAddress(const MCAsmInfo *MAI, unsigned Base, 0
904 const MCOperand &DispMO, unsigned Index, ----
905 raw_ostream &OS) { ----
906 printOperand(DispMO, MAI, OS); 0
907 if (Base || Index) { 0
908 OS << '('; 0
909 if (Index) { 0
910 printFormattedRegName(MAI, Index, OS); 0
911 if (Base) 0
912 OS << ','; 0
913 } ----
914 if (Base) 0
915 printFormattedRegName(MAI, Base, OS); 0
916 OS << ')'; 0
917 } ----
918 } 0
919 ----
920 bool SystemZAsmPrinter::PrintAsmOperand(const MachineInstr *MI, unsigned OpNo, 0
921 const char *ExtraCode, ----
922 raw_ostream &OS) { ----
923 const MCRegisterInfo &MRI = *TM.getMCRegisterInfo(); 0
924 const MachineOperand &MO = MI->getOperand(OpNo); 0
925 MCOperand MCOp; 0
926 if (ExtraCode) { 0
927 if (ExtraCode[0] == 'N' && !ExtraCode[1] && MO.isReg() && 0
928 SystemZ::GR128BitRegClass.contains(MO.getReg())) 0
929 MCOp = ----
930 MCOperand::createReg(MRI.getSubReg(MO.getReg(), SystemZ::subreg_l64)); 0
931 else ----
932 return AsmPrinter::PrintAsmOperand(MI, OpNo, ExtraCode, OS); 0
933 } else { ----
934 SystemZMCInstLower Lower(MF->getContext(), *this); 0
935 MCOp = Lower.lowerOperand(MO); 0
936 } ----
937 printOperand(MCOp, MAI, OS); 0
938 return false; 0
939 } ----
940 ----
941 bool SystemZAsmPrinter::PrintAsmMemoryOperand(const MachineInstr *MI, 0
942 unsigned OpNo, ----
943 const char *ExtraCode, ----
944 raw_ostream &OS) { ----
945 printAddress(MAI, MI->getOperand(OpNo).getReg(), 0
946 MCOperand::createImm(MI->getOperand(OpNo + 1).getImm()), 0
947 MI->getOperand(OpNo + 2).getReg(), OS); 0
948 return false; 0
949 } ----

951 void SystemZAsmPrinter::emitEndOfAsmFile(Module &M) { 0
952 auto TT = OutContext.getTargetTriple(); 0
953 if (TT.isOSzOS()) { 0
954 emitADASection(); 0
955 } ----
956 emitAttributes(M); 0
957 } 0
958 ----
959 void SystemZAsmPrinter::emitADASection() { 0
960 OutStreamer->pushSection(); 0
961 ----
962 const unsigned PointerSize = getDataLayout().getPointerSize(); 0
963 OutStreamer->switchSection(getObjFileLowering().getADASection()); 0
964 ----
965 unsigned EmittedBytes = 0; 0
966 for (auto &Entry : ADATable.getTable()) { 0
967 const MCSymbol *Sym; ----
968 unsigned SlotKind; ----
969 std::tie(Sym, SlotKind) = Entry.first; 0
970 unsigned Offset = Entry.second; 0
971 assert(Offset == EmittedBytes && "Offset not as expected"); 0
972 (void)EmittedBytes; ----
973 #define EMIT_COMMENT(Str) \ ----
974 OutStreamer->AddComment(Twine("Offset ") \ ----
975 .concat(utostr(Offset)) \ ----
976 .concat(" " Str " ") \ ----
977 .concat(Sym->getName())); ----
978 switch (SlotKind) { 0
979 case SystemZII::MO_ADA_DIRECT_FUNC_DESC: 0
980 // Language Environment DLL logic requires function descriptors, for ----
981 // imported functions, that are placed in the ADA to be 8 byte aligned. ----
982 EMIT_COMMENT("function descriptor of"); 0
983 OutStreamer->emitValue( 0
984 SystemZMCExpr::create(SystemZMCExpr::VK_SystemZ_RCon, 0
985 MCSymbolRefExpr::create(Sym, OutContext), 0
986 OutContext), ----
987 PointerSize); ----
988 OutStreamer->emitValue( 0
989 SystemZMCExpr::create(SystemZMCExpr::VK_SystemZ_VCon, 0
990 MCSymbolRefExpr::create(Sym, OutContext), 0
991 OutContext), ----
992 PointerSize); ----
993 EmittedBytes += PointerSize * 2; 0
994 break; 0
995 case SystemZII::MO_ADA_DATA_SYMBOL_ADDR: 0
996 EMIT_COMMENT("pointer to data symbol"); 0
997 OutStreamer->emitValue( 0
998 SystemZMCExpr::create(SystemZMCExpr::VK_SystemZ_None, 0
999 MCSymbolRefExpr::create(Sym, OutContext), 0
1000 OutContext), ----
1001 PointerSize); ----
1002 EmittedBytes += PointerSize; 0
1003 break; 0
1004 case SystemZII::MO_ADA_INDIRECT_FUNC_DESC: { 0
1005 MCSymbol *Alias = OutContext.createTempSymbol( 0
1006 Twine(Sym->getName()).concat("@indirect")); 0
1007 OutStreamer->emitAssignment(Alias, 0
1008 MCSymbolRefExpr::create(Sym, OutContext)); 0
1009 OutStreamer->emitSymbolAttribute(Alias, MCSA_IndirectSymbol); 0
1010 ----
1011 EMIT_COMMENT("pointer to function descriptor"); 0
1012 OutStreamer->emitValue( 0
1013 SystemZMCExpr::create(SystemZMCExpr::VK_SystemZ_VCon, 0
1014 MCSymbolRefExpr::create(Alias, OutContext), 0
1015 OutContext), ----
1016 PointerSize); ----
1017 EmittedBytes += PointerSize; 0
1018 break; 0
1019 } ----
1020 default: 0
1021 llvm_unreachable("Unexpected slot kind"); 0
1022 } ----
1023 #undef EMIT_COMMENT ----
1024 } ----
1025 OutStreamer->popSection(); 0
1026 } 0
1027 ----
1028 void SystemZAsmPrinter::emitFunctionBodyEnd() { 0
1029 if (TM.getTargetTriple().isOSzOS()) { 0
1030 // Emit symbol for the end of function if the z/OS target streamer ----
1031 // is used. This is needed to calculate the size of the function. ----
1032 MCSymbol *FnEndSym = createTempSymbol("func_end"); 0
1033 OutStreamer->emitLabel(FnEndSym); 0
1034 ----
1035 OutStreamer->pushSection(); 0
1036 OutStreamer->switchSection(getObjFileLowering().getPPA1Section()); 0
1037 emitPPA1(FnEndSym); 0
1038 OutStreamer->popSection(); 0
1039 ----
1040 CurrentFnPPA1Sym = nullptr; 0
1041 CurrentFnEPMarkerSym = nullptr; 0
1042 } ----
1043 } 0
1044 ----
1045 static void emitPPA1Flags(std::unique_ptr &OutStreamer, bool VarArg, 0
1046 bool StackProtector, bool FPRMask, bool VRMask) { ----
1047 enum class PPA1Flag1 : uint8_t { ----
1048 DSA64Bit = (0x80 >> 0), ----
1049 VarArg = (0x80 >> 7), ----
1050 LLVM_MARK_AS_BITMASK_ENUM(DSA64Bit) ----
1051 }; ----
1052 enum class PPA1Flag2 : uint8_t { ----
1053 ExternalProcedure = (0x80 >> 0), ----
1054 STACKPROTECTOR = (0x80 >> 3), ----
1055 LLVM_MARK_AS_BITMASK_ENUM(ExternalProcedure) ----
1056 }; ----
1057 enum class PPA1Flag3 : uint8_t { ----
1058 FPRMask = (0x80 >> 2), ----
1059 LLVM_MARK_AS_BITMASK_ENUM(FPRMask) ----
1060 }; ----
1061 enum class PPA1Flag4 : uint8_t { ----
1062 EPMOffsetPresent = (0x80 >> 0), ----
1063 VRMask = (0x80 >> 2), ----
1064 ProcedureNamePresent = (0x80 >> 7), ----
1065 LLVM_MARK_AS_BITMASK_ENUM(EPMOffsetPresent) ----
1066 }; ----
1067 ----
1068 // Declare optional section flags that can be modified. ----
1069 auto Flags1 = PPA1Flag1(0); 0
1070 auto Flags2 = PPA1Flag2::ExternalProcedure; 0
1071 auto Flags3 = PPA1Flag3(0); 0
1072 auto Flags4 = PPA1Flag4::EPMOffsetPresent | PPA1Flag4::ProcedureNamePresent; 0
1073 ----
1074 Flags1 |= PPA1Flag1::DSA64Bit; 0
1075 ----
1076 if (VarArg) 0
1077 Flags1 |= PPA1Flag1::VarArg; 0
1078 ----
1079 if (StackProtector) 0
1080 Flags2 |= PPA1Flag2::STACKPROTECTOR; 0
1081 ----
1082 // SavedGPRMask, SavedFPRMask, and SavedVRMask are precomputed in. ----
1083 if (FPRMask) 0
1084 Flags3 |= PPA1Flag3::FPRMask; // Add emit FPR mask flag. 0
1085 ----
1086 if (VRMask) 0
1087 Flags4 |= PPA1Flag4::VRMask; // Add emit VR mask flag. 0
1088 ----
1089 OutStreamer->AddComment("PPA1 Flags 1"); 0
1090 if ((Flags1 & PPA1Flag1::DSA64Bit) == PPA1Flag1::DSA64Bit) 0
1091 OutStreamer->AddComment(" Bit 0: 1 = 64-bit DSA"); 0
1092 else ----
1093 OutStreamer->AddComment(" Bit 0: 0 = 32-bit DSA"); 0
1094 if ((Flags1 & PPA1Flag1::VarArg) == PPA1Flag1::VarArg) 0
1095 OutStreamer->AddComment(" Bit 7: 1 = Vararg function"); 0
1096 OutStreamer->emitInt8(static_cast(Flags1)); // Flags 1. 0
1097 ----
1098 OutStreamer->AddComment("PPA1 Flags 2"); 0
1099 if ((Flags2 & PPA1Flag2::ExternalProcedure) == PPA1Flag2::ExternalProcedure) 0
1100 OutStreamer->AddComment(" Bit 0: 1 = External procedure"); 0
1101 if ((Flags2 & PPA1Flag2::STACKPROTECTOR) == PPA1Flag2::STACKPROTECTOR) 0
1102 OutStreamer->AddComment(" Bit 3: 1 = STACKPROTECT is enabled"); 0
1103 else ----
1104 OutStreamer->AddComment(" Bit 3: 0 = STACKPROTECT is not enabled"); 0
1105 OutStreamer->emitInt8(static_cast(Flags2)); // Flags 2. 0
1106 ----
1107 OutStreamer->AddComment("PPA1 Flags 3"); 0
1108 if ((Flags3 & PPA1Flag3::FPRMask) == PPA1Flag3::FPRMask) 0
1109 OutStreamer->AddComment(" Bit 2: 1 = FP Reg Mask is in optional area"); 0
1110 OutStreamer->emitInt8( 0
1111 static_cast(Flags3)); // Flags 3 (optional sections). ----
1112 ----
1113 OutStreamer->AddComment("PPA1 Flags 4"); 0
1114 if ((Flags4 & PPA1Flag4::VRMask) == PPA1Flag4::VRMask) 0
1115 OutStreamer->AddComment(" Bit 2: 1 = Vector Reg Mask is in optional area"); 0
1116 OutStreamer->emitInt8(static_cast( 0
1117 Flags4)); // Flags 4 (optional sections, always emit these). ----
1118 } 0
1119 ----
1120 void SystemZAsmPrinter::emitPPA1(MCSymbol *FnEndSym) { 0
1121 const TargetRegisterInfo *TRI = MF->getRegInfo().getTargetRegisterInfo(); 0
1122 const SystemZSubtarget &Subtarget = MF->getSubtarget(); 0
1123 const auto TargetHasVector = Subtarget.hasVector(); 0
1124 ----
1125 const SystemZMachineFunctionInfo *ZFI = ----
1126 MF->getInfo(); 0
1127 const auto *ZFL = static_cast( ----
1128 Subtarget.getFrameLowering()); 0
1129 const MachineFrameInfo &MFFrame = MF->getFrameInfo(); 0
1130 ----
1131 // Get saved GPR/FPR/VPR masks. ----
1132 const std::vector &CSI = MFFrame.getCalleeSavedInfo(); 0
1133 uint16_t SavedGPRMask = 0; 0
1134 uint16_t SavedFPRMask = 0; 0
1135 uint8_t SavedVRMask = 0; 0
1136 int64_t OffsetFPR = 0; 0
1137 int64_t OffsetVR = 0; 0
1138 const int64_t TopOfStack = ----
1139 MFFrame.getOffsetAdjustment() + MFFrame.getStackSize(); 0
1140 ----
1141 // Loop over the spilled registers. The CalleeSavedInfo can't be used because ----
1142 // it does not contain all spilled registers. ----
1143 for (unsigned I = ZFI->getSpillGPRRegs().LowGPR, 0
1144 E = ZFI->getSpillGPRRegs().HighGPR; 0
1145 I && E && I <= E; ++I) { 0
1146 unsigned V = TRI->getEncodingValue((Register)I); 0
1147 assert(V < 16 && "GPR index out of range"); 0
1148 SavedGPRMask |= 1 << (15 - V); 0
1149 } ----
1150 ----
1151 for (auto &CS : CSI) { 0
1152 unsigned Reg = CS.getReg(); 0
